Select, Create, and Synthesise all aspects of Stage 1 The Scoping Exercise.  Stage 1 of the DSAT Training Needs Analysis (TNA) focuses on defining the training requirement by identifying the performance gap between current and desired capabilities.   This involves analyzing the operational role, identifying tasks that need to be performed, and determining whether training is the appropriate solution.   Key activities include stakeholder consultation, reviewing doctrine and policy, and establishing training objectives.   The outcome of this stage is a clear definition of the training requirement, forming the foundation for subsequent analysis and design phases in the DSAT process.
